function test()
local time_m = level.get_time_minutes()
local time_h = level.get_time_hours()
if not time_h == 5 and not time_m == 32 and has_alife_info("trade_up") then
db.actor:disable_info_portion("trade_up")
elseif time_h == 5 and time_m == 32 and not has_alife_info("trade_up") then
db.actor:give_info_portion("trade_up")
end
end

function main()
  for a=1,65535,1 do
  local obj=level.object_by_id(a)
    if obj and string.find(obj:name(),"esc_wolf_respawn") then
    local state = state_mgr.get_state(obj)
    local offset = vector():set(math.random() * 2 - 1, 0, math.random() * 2 - 1)
offset:normalize()
local dist = db.actor:position():distance_to(obj:position())
    local vertex_id = level.vertex_in_direction(db.actor:level_vertex_id(), offset, 4.0)
  if state_lib.states[state].movement ~= move.stand and dist > 3.0 then
    utils.send_to_nearest_accessible_vertex(obj, vertex_id)
  end
    end
  end
end

function main()
local sobj = alife():object("esc_wolf")
local obj = level.object_by_id(sobj.id)
local vertex_id = level.vertex_in_direction(db.actor:level_vertex_id(),vector():set(0,0,0),4)
state_mgr.set_state(obj,"sprint",nil,nil,nil)
obj:set_desired_position()
obj:set_desired_direction()
obj:set_detail_path_type(move.line)
obj:set_path_type(game_object.level_path)
utils.send_to_nearest_accessible_vertex(obj,vertex_id)
end

-- –æ—Ç–æ—Å–ª–∞—Ç—å –≤ –±–ª–∏–∂–∞–π—à—É—é —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à—ë–Ω–Ω—É—é –Ω–æ–¥—É –ø–æ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—é –∫ –∑–∞–¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–π.
-- –≤–æ–∑–≤—Ä–∞—â–∞–µ—Ç vertex_id, –≤ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–µ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª –ø–µ—Ä—Å–æ–Ω–∞–∂–∞
function send_to_nearest_accessible_vertex( npc, v_id )
  if not npc:accessible( v_id ) then
    local vtemp = vector()
    v_id, vtemp = npc:accessible_nearest( level.vertex_position( v_id ), vtemp )
  end

  npc:set_dest_level_vertex_id( v_id )

  return v_id
end

function main()
local sobj = alife():object("esc_wolf")
local obj = level.object_by_id(sobj.id)
local vertex_id = level.vertex_in_direction(db.actor:level_vertex_id(),vector():set(0,0,0),4)
state_mgr.set_state(obj,"sprint",nil,nil,nil)
obj:set_desired_position()
obj:set_desired_direction()
obj:set_detail_path_type(move.line)
obj:set_path_type(game_object.level_path)
utils.send_to_nearest_accessible_vertex(obj,vertex_id)
end
